      <script type="text/javascript">
       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_2615592").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/2615592?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_2615592").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_2615592").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_2615592").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}
      </script>

    var themeActionsBanner = null;
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		themeActionsBanner = jQuery("#theme-actions-banner");
		jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
			if(parseInt(jQuery(this).scrollTop(), 10) &gt; 51) {
				themeActionsBanner.addClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "41px");
			} else {
				themeActionsBanner.removeClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "10px");
			}
		});
	});
   </script>

    var logoContainer;
		var infosContainer;
		var logoToHome;
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			logoContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-logo");
			infosContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-infos");

			logoToHome = jQuery("#logoToHome", logoContainer);
			//makes the logo Rumble
			logoToHome.jrumble({
				x: 0,
				y: 0,
				rotation: 4,
				speed: 75
			});
			logoToHome.hover(function() {
				var logo = $(this);
				logo.trigger('startRumble');
				// Stop 500ms after
				setTimeout(function() {
					logo.trigger('stopRumble');
				}, 500);
			}, function(){
				$(this).trigger('stopRumble');
			});
		});

             <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4038568341">
              <h1 class="h2 postTitleView" itemprop="name">
               <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://blog.toasttab.com/emv-what-restaurants-need-to-know-before-october-2015-deadline?success=true" onclick="trackPostClick(4038568341 ,{addClick:'popupPostClickOnTitle', hasRelatedPosts: 'false'}); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                EMV: What Restaurants Need to Know Before the October 2015 Deadline
               </a>
              </h1>
             </div>
             <div class="post-content clearfix ">
              <div class="post-image">
               <a href="http://blog.toasttab.com/emv-what-restaurants-need-to-know-before-october-2015-deadline?success=true" onclick="trackPostClick(4038568341,{addClick:'popupPostClickOnImage', hasRelatedPosts: 'false'}); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                <div class="thisistherealimage">
                 <img alt="EMV: What Restaurants Need to Know Before the October 2015 Deadline | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="345" id="postImage_4038568341" itemprop="image" src="http://img.scoop.it/JjDv0-xSJytUy0GRjUIb5Dl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 345;" width="467"/>
                </div>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
               From
               <a href="http://blog.toasttab.com/emv-what-restaurants-need-to-know-before-october-2015-deadline?success=true" onclick="trackPostClick(4038568341,{addClick:'popupPostClickOnDomain', hasRelatedPosts: 'false'}); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

               <span>

              <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
               <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4038568341" itemprop="description">
                <p>
                 <span>
                  If you havent heard about EMV payments, thats because the United States has been notoriously slow to embrace EMV security standards compared to other parts of the world. That said, restaurant owners and other merchants should expect the transition to EMV technology to speed up drastically in 2015.
                 </span>
                </p>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047592535">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/elephant-bar-increases-customer-visits-130000568.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4047592535 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Elephant Bar Increases Customer Visits With Paytronix Geofencing Campaigns
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/elephant-bar-increases-customer-visits-130000568.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4047592535); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Elephant Bar Increases Customer Visits With Paytronix Geofencing Campaigns | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="82" id="postImage_4047592535" src="http://img.scoop.it/uLDdy4NLfpX79f6dUuKp2Dl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:112; height: 82;" width="112"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://finance.yahoo.com/news/elephant-bar-increases-customer-visits-130000568.html" onclick="trackPostClick(4047592535); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   finance
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .yahoo
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047592535/2015/07/13/elephant-bar-increases-customer-visits-with-paytronix-geofencing-campaigns">
                    Today, 1:33 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047592535">
                   <blockquote>
                    Paytronix Systems, Inc., a leading provider of reward program solutions to restaurants and retailers, today announced that the Elephant Bar restaurant chain has successfully deployed its geofencing capability. These messages compel visits from Elephant Bar Rewards members when they are within a set proximity to a restaurant. In a review of three recent campaigns, Elephant Bar determined that approximately 30% of members visited a restaurant on the day that they received a geofencing message.
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                   <span>
                    Latest technology can fire the order to the kitchen based on the guests anticipated arrivial time from their physical lacation and notifies staff when guests arrive, this is very cool technology!
                   </span>

                    Who provides this technology?

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047583874">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.singleplatform.com/2015/07/07/customer-loyalty-programs-three-reasons-why-they-matter-to-your-restaurant-or-small-business/?hootPostID=8d3ddfaecf05069999aa32a2c946b035" onclick="trackPostClick(4047583874 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Customer Loyalty Programs: Three reasons why they matter to your restaurant or small business
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.singleplatform.com/2015/07/07/customer-loyalty-programs-three-reasons-why-they-matter-to-your-restaurant-or-small-business/?hootPostID=8d3ddfaecf05069999aa32a2c946b035" onclick="trackPostClick(4047583874); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Customer Loyalty Programs: Three reasons why they matter to your restaurant or small business | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="367" id="postImage_4047583874" src="http://img.scoop.it/Lhp-S_bRomaulUaIITF8PDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 367;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.singleplatform.com/2015/07/07/customer-loyalty-programs-three-reasons-why-they-matter-to-your-restaurant-or-small-business/?hootPostID=8d3ddfaecf05069999aa32a2c946b035" onclick="trackPostClick(4047583874); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .singleplatform
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047583874/2015/07/13/customer-loyalty-programs-three-reasons-why-they-matter-to-your-restaurant-or-small-business">
                    Today, 10:08 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047583874">
                   <blockquote>
                    80% of your business revenuecomes from just 20% of your customers, and it costs your business6-7 times moreto attract a new customer than it does to keep an existing one. Taking a look at these statistics, the importance of establishing a customer base and learning what it takes to satisfy them is crucial in not only increasing your revenue, but also in saving your business money.
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://smartblogs.com/food-and-beverage/2015/07/10/we-need-to-build-a-mobile-app-agencies-and-utilities-vs-frameworks/" onclick="trackPostClick(4047435853 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   How restaurant brands can build a mobile app with purpose
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://smartblogs.com/food-and-beverage/2015/07/10/we-need-to-build-a-mobile-app-agencies-and-utilities-vs-frameworks/" onclick="trackPostClick(4047435853); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="How restaurant brands can build a mobile app with purpose | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="149" id="postImage_4047435853" src="http://img.scoop.it/hPq7gYR7PmXDY9sIvJ8GxTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 149;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://smartblogs.com/food-and-beverage/2015/07/10/we-need-to-build-a-mobile-app-agencies-and-utilities-vs-frameworks/" onclick="trackPostClick(4047435853); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047435853">
                   <blockquote>
                    The smartphone is so much more than a screen or a replacement for a plastic card or a sheet of paper. The smartphone is identifiable, contactable, interactive, web-enabled, location-aware and commerce-ready. The smartphone provides restaurant brands with a new way to do business with their loyal guests, enabling greater hospitality through enhanced service models that make the guest experience faster, more accurate, and more personal. The smartphone empowers the guest to order and pay from everywhere and the restaurant to accept orders and payments from everywhere.
                   </blockquote>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047241245">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="https://medium.com/tech-trends-for-restaurant/how-restaurants-can-use-pre-orders-for-lunch-to-attract-busy-people-df1162dd3184" onclick="trackPostClick(4047241245 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   How Restaurants Can Use Pre-Orders for Lunch to Attract Busy People
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-htmlfragment htmlfragment">
                  <script async="" src="https://static.medium.com/embed.js">
                  </script>
                  <a class="m-story" data-collapsed="true" href="https://medium.com/tech-trends-for-restaurant/how-restaurants-can-use-pre-orders-for-lunch-to-attract-busy-people-df1162dd3184">
                   How Restaurants Can Use Pre-Orders for Lunch to Attract Busy People - Tech Trends For Restaurant - Medium
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="https://medium.com/tech-trends-for-restaurant/how-restaurants-can-use-pre-orders-for-lunch-to-attract-busy-people-df1162dd3184" onclick="trackPostClick(4047241245); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   medium
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047241245/2015/07/07/how-restaurants-can-use-pre-orders-for-lunch-to-attract-busy-people">
                    July 7, 5:48 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047241245">
                   <p>
                    Do you serve lunches immediately after your guests arrive? Because a lot of busy dinersentrepreneurs, app developers and other career-oriented folkswould like you do so.Surveys show that guests expect restaurants to use more technology and Allset is the newest such service. Its a reservation appfor iPhone and Androidthat lets guests book tables and pre-order lunches at participating restaurants. The special thing about Allset is table booking+food pre-ordering approach. Usually restaurants use different services to accept reservations and orders. Allset put two technologies in one app.
                   </p>
                  </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://loyalty360.org/resources/article/twin-peaks-sparks-greater-customer-engagement" onclick="trackPostClick(4047206175 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Twin Peaks Looks to Mobile Technology to Spark Greater Customer Engagement
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://loyalty360.org/resources/article/twin-peaks-sparks-greater-customer-engagement" onclick="trackPostClick(4047206175); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Twin Peaks Looks to Mobile Technology to Spark Greater Customer Engagement | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="336" id="postImage_4047206175" src="http://img.scoop.it/aHM5W2UmNsnyCthlPQkCnzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 336;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://loyalty360.org/resources/article/twin-peaks-sparks-greater-customer-engagement" onclick="trackPostClick(4047206175); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .org
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047206175/2015/07/07/twin-peaks-looks-to-mobile-technology-to-spark-greater-customer-engagement">
                    July 7, 4:13 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047206175">
                   <p>
                    Twin Peaks, a national restaurant chain with 68 locations in 24 states, is looking to enhance its customer engagement via mobile payment app technology.The new Twin Peaks mobile app will allow customers to view, split, and pay their bills from their phones using Apple Pay, PayPal, Google Wallet, debit or credit cards; order additional menu items, and access exclusive rewards and special offers only redeemable in the app.
                   </p>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047084046">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.nightclub.com/growing-sales/social-media-marketing/5-ways-refresh-your-summer-social-media-strategy" onclick="trackPostClick(4047084046 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   5 Ways to Refresh Your Restaurant's Social Media Strategy for the Summer
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.nightclub.com/growing-sales/social-media-marketing/5-ways-refresh-your-summer-social-media-strategy" onclick="trackPostClick(4047084046); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="5 Ways to Refresh Your Restaurant's Social Media Strategy for the Summer | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="224" id="postImage_4047084046" src="http://img.scoop.it/22X1C8Mb-3h3_kVCmekGhjl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 224;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.nightclub.com/growing-sales/social-media-marketing/5-ways-refresh-your-summer-social-media-strategy" onclick="trackPostClick(4047084046); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .nightclub
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047084046/2015/07/05/5-ways-to-refresh-your-restaurant-s-social-media-strategy-for-the-summer">
                    July 5, 8:24 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047084046">
                   <blockquote>
                    Summer is here and the living - should you be lucky enough to be doing business in a resort or vacation community - may be easy. However, your venue may be located in a city or a college town and the weekends have suddenly become lonely and sad, as your regular customers escape to the shore, the mountains or other places with umbrella drinks. If youre busy, summer is a great time to capture memories via social media and keep the buzz alive into the fall and winter. If youre slow, use the time to learn more about digital marketing and plan your strategy for the months ahead. Here are five tips that will keep your business hot this summer.
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                   <span>
                    Restaurant marketing is all about Social Media and you can't afford to miss a single review or chance to reply to a customer or critic's comment!Social Media Marketing is an every day event, make sure your restaurant is updating your Social Media accounts and blogging every day.
                   </span>
                   <span>
                   </span>
                   <span>
                    For a weekly recap of restaurant industry and Social Media news, ideas and articles, subscribe to the weekly "
                   </span>

                    Restaurant Newsletter
                   </a>
                   <span>
                    " delivered free via email every Tuesday at
                   </span>
                   <a href="http://pos-advicenewsletter.com/" rel="nofollow">
                    http://pos-advicenewsletter.com/
                   </a>
                  </p>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://restaurantengine.com/restaurant-improve-its-systems/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046944239 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Where Can Your Restaurant Improve Its Systems?
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://restaurantengine.com/restaurant-improve-its-systems/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046944239); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Where Can Your Restaurant Improve Its Systems? | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="478" id="postImage_4046944239" src="http://img.scoop.it/bwFaw_PhuOP5_Y3Kg9bx7zl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 478;" width="467"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://restaurantengine.com/restaurant-improve-its-systems/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046944239); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   restaurantengine

                   </wbr>

                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046944239/2015/07/02/where-can-your-restaurant-improve-its-systems">
                    July 2, 5:52 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046944239">
                   <p>
                    Your restaurant is a microcosm of systems. All of these systems should work together to produce the end result: great food, comfortable ambiance and incredible service.Have you ever thought about improving some of these systems? Even though they may be working just fine, are they working as good as they could be?Is there room for improvement that could eventually lead to better results or a more efficient overall process?
                   </p>

             <div class="post onePost ">
              <div class="clear">
              </div>
              <div class="ugc" data-lid="4046750180" data-tlid="2615592" data-viewmode="" id="post_4046750180">
               <div class="post-from postFrom">
                <table class="post-history posthistory">
                 <tr>
                  <td class="post-from-avatar">
                   <a class=" preview-profile" href="http://www.scoop.it/u/bob-frazier">
                    <img class="avatar" src="http://img.scoop.it/1m1cpxePwyk7IgMSff_0z-y7_ZqweuUDvdarVjaIR5c="/>

               <div class="post-view postView post-embed left medium ">
                <div class="rescoop-container">
                 <div class="rescoop">
                  <div class="button button-rescoop default " onclick="showSignupPopup(null, null, '?rescoop=4046750180');return false;" x-data-rescoop-onclick="showPostInScoopitWindow('/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046750180/2015/06/29/mobile-payments-loyalty-create-new-avenues-for-fraud-at-restaurants/rescoop/2', null)">
                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>
                   <span>
                    Scoop.it!
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046750180">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/magazine/june-2015/mobile-payments---loyalty-create-new-avenues-for-fraud100544?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046750180 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Mobile Payments &amp; Loyalty Create New Avenues for Fraud at Restaurants
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/magazine/june-2015/mobile-payments---loyalty-create-new-avenues-for-fraud100544?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046750180); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Mobile Payments &amp; Loyalty Create New Avenues for Fraud at Restaurants | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="247" id="postImage_4046750180" src="http://img.scoop.it/Jr3pg_OHZ4SuOZ4iODYCTjl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 247;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/magazine/june-2015/mobile-payments---loyalty-create-new-avenues-for-fraud100544?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046750180); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   hospitalitytechno
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   logy
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .edgl
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046750180/2015/06/29/mobile-payments-loyalty-create-new-avenues-for-fraud-at-restaurants">
                    June 29, 2:35 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046750180">
                   <p>
                    When it comes to loss prevention in restaurants, threats come from many areas: operators worry about the physical safety of employees and guests, stolen or spoiled inventory, and both internal and external theft. Now, with the introduction of new technologies, a fresh landscape of threats is developing that can lead to profit loss if operators are not vigilant.The [restaurant] industry doesnt see as much shrink as the retail side, but with mobile payments, loyalty programs or gift cards using apps, restaurants need to be more protective of fraud, says Jim Forlenza, executive director of the Restaurant Loss Prevention and Security Association (
                    <a href="http://www.rlpsa.com" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     www.rlpsa.com
                    </a>
                    ). HT takes a look at three areas that can pose potential fraud risks for operators and offers precautions.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046448029">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.paymentssource.com/news/retail-acquiring/few-merchants-will-be-emv-compliant-in-october-javelin-3021650-1.html?ET=paymentssource%3Ae4988932%3Aa%3A&amp;st=email" onclick="trackPostClick(4046448029 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Barely 25% of Merchants Will Be EMV Complaint October 1st
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.paymentssource.com/news/retail-acquiring/few-merchants-will-be-emv-compliant-in-october-javelin-3021650-1.html?ET=paymentssource%3Ae4988932%3Aa%3A&amp;st=email" onclick="trackPostClick(4046448029); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Barely 25% of Merchants Will Be EMV Complaint October 1st | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="143" id="postImage_4046448029" src="http://img.scoop.it/1kgOPPYwwHBpeJJiaC9y9Tl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 143;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.paymentssource.com/news/retail-acquiring/few-merchants-will-be-emv-compliant-in-october-javelin-3021650-1.html?ET=paymentssource%3Ae4988932%3Aa%3A&amp;st=email" onclick="trackPostClick(4046448029); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .paymentssource
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046448029/2015/06/24/barely-25-of-merchants-will-be-emv-complaint-october-1st">
                    June 24, 3:51 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046448029">
                   <p>
                    Although it's been widely suspected that merchant EMV compliance will be low in October when the liability shift deadline kicks in, a new Javelin Strategy &amp; Researchreport is projecting as many as 75% of all merchants will not make the deadline.The smaller merchants are clearly not ready, not by a longshot," said Nick Holland, Javelin's payments director. "The majority of small merchants are not only not ready for EMV, they are not even aware of EMV."
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">

                    <a href="http://sco.lt/4wjVZJ" rel="nofollow">
                     EMV video
                    </a>
                    at
                    <a href="http://sco.lt/4wjVZJ" rel="nofollow">
                     http://sco.lt/4wjVZJ
                    </a>
                    and here is a link to another
                    <a href="http://sco.lt/88K2in" rel="nofollow">
                     EMV article
                    </a>
                    at.
                    <a href="http://sco.lt/88K2in" rel="nofollow">
                     http://sco.lt/88K2in
                    </a>
                    .Are you ready for the 10/1/15 liability shift?Restaurateurs can
                    <strong>
                     Find, Compare and Connect
                    </strong>
                    with EMV and mobile payment solutions and providers at
                    <a href="http://restaurantsoftwarelist.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                     the Restaurant Software List website
                    </a>
                    at
                    <a href="http://www.restaurantsoftwarelist.com/" rel="nofollow">
                     http://www.restaurantsoftwarelist.com/
                    </a>

                    </a>
                   </p>

                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.digitalsignagetoday.com/blogs/restaurant-digital-signage-is-heating-up/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046437811); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Restaurant digital signage is heating up | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="126" id="postImage_4046437811" src="http://img.scoop.it/si56Nj9Q4y_vHwSp0MD1GDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 126;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.digitalsignagetoday.com/blogs/restaurant-digital-signage-is-heating-up/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046437811); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .digitalsignagetod
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   ay
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046437811/2015/06/24/restaurant-digital-signage-is-heating-up">
                    June 24, 11:35 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046437811">
                   <p>
                    Test data that proves the value of digital menu boards has been available for several years. However, you have to take advantage of the many features of the digital menu boards in order to obtain their full value.I say that because, for various reasons, restaurant chains have been very slow to take advantage of many of the primary features of digital menu boards.Even some of the major chains that have rolled out indoor digital menu boards continue to use them much the sameas they did their old-style boards. They have not used the additional features to their full extent. This can be very frustrating to me because I've been in the digital menu board business for so long assisting in the development of these features.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://blog.mry.com/2015/06/19/leveraging-location-how-geo-tags-are-changing-the-restaurant-game/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046288888 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Leveraging Location: How Geo-Tags are Changing the Restaurant Game
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://blog.mry.com/2015/06/19/leveraging-location-how-geo-tags-are-changing-the-restaurant-game/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046288888); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Leveraging Location: How Geo-Tags are Changing the Restaurant Game | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="200" id="postImage_4046288888" src="http://img.scoop.it/HO8Wfwh-FF2--Rmzl1hiazl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:112; height: 200;" width="112"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://blog.mry.com/2015/06/19/leveraging-location-how-geo-tags-are-changing-the-restaurant-game/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046288888); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046288888">
                   <blockquote>
                    Foodstagraming has been around for as long as photo filters like Nashville and Kelvin have existed, but no longer are food bloggers the only ones taking their foodie feeds to the next level. Hashtags like #foodporn, #foodgasm, and #instafood link to tens of millions of photos shared by countless users. Everyone from famous athletes and fashion bloggers to your parents are snapping pictures of their favorite restaurant eats. Even those who disparage foodstagraming find it hard to resist scrolling endlessly through the abundance of mouthwatering photographs.
                   </blockquote>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046048773">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.restaurantbusinessonline.com/news/nyc-looks-halt-use-tech-underreport-restaurant-sales?spMailingID=48848380&amp;spUserID=MTQwMjMzNDUwOTE1S0&amp;spJobID=701296092&amp;spReportId=NzAxMjk2MDkyS0" onclick="trackPostClick(4046048773 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   NYC looks to halt use of tech to underreport restaurant POS sales
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.restaurantbusinessonline.com/news/nyc-looks-halt-use-tech-underreport-restaurant-sales?spMailingID=48848380&amp;spUserID=MTQwMjMzNDUwOTE1S0&amp;spJobID=701296092&amp;spReportId=NzAxMjk2MDkyS0" onclick="trackPostClick(4046048773); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="NYC looks to halt use of tech to underreport restaurant POS sales | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="169" id="postImage_4046048773" src="http://img.scoop.it/jYqTfQZqVwzx43gZ2Iz9iTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 169;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.restaurantbusinessonline.com/news/nyc-looks-halt-use-tech-underreport-restaurant-sales?spMailingID=48848380&amp;spUserID=MTQwMjMzNDUwOTE1S0&amp;spJobID=701296092&amp;spReportId=NzAxMjk2MDkyS0" onclick="trackPostClick(4046048773); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .restaurantbusines
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   sonline
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046048773/2015/06/18/nyc-looks-to-halt-use-of-tech-to-underreport-restaurant-pos-sales">
                    June 18, 1:01 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046048773">
                   <p>
                    Seven restaurants have already admitted to using the devices to evade $2 million in sales taxes, according to a report drafted by a New York State Supreme Court Grand Jury.Sales tax evasion is nothing new, but software that helps unscrupulous merchants commit fraud is, Manhattan District Attorney Cyrus Vance, Jr., said in a statement. The pressures on the citys restaurant industry  skyrocketing rents, labor costs, food commodity pricing fluctuations, and intense competition  make it especially vulnerable.Vance indicated that he intends to employ recommendations in the Grand Jury report to halt the use of the gizmos, which prompt POS systems not to record transactions. The devices are not illegal in New York state, though their use for tax evasion is.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">

                  <p>
                   Skimmers have been around for years, but their useage has declined since many states hold both the merchant and the vendor accountable!

                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://techcrunch.com/2015/07/11/the-billion-dollar-food-delivery-wars/?mc_cid=ff6f235e8d&amp;mc_eid=1dd8be872d" onclick="trackPostClick(4047584056); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="The Billion Dollar Food DeliveryWars | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="351" id="postImage_4047584056" src="http://img.scoop.it/wamCxP5gtJTandgv_FUTuzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:467; height: 351;" width="467"/>

                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047584056">
                   <p>
                    Over the past 12 months, food and grocery delivery has been one of the hottest VC sectors. More than $1 billion was invested in 2014  an almost fourfold increase year-on-year  with a further half a billion dollars invested in Q1 2015,according to CB Insights.Since the successful IPOs of Just Eat and Grubhub/Seamless a year ago, almost every week has brought fresh news of large-scale funding announcements for existing players, or the launch of a new service, making it one of the most competitive sectors currently.
                   </p>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.cutimes.com/2015/07/05/data-breaches-on-record-pace-for-2015" onclick="trackPostClick(4047368743 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Data Breaches on Record Pace for 2015
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.cutimes.com/2015/07/05/data-breaches-on-record-pace-for-2015" onclick="trackPostClick(4047368743); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Data Breaches on Record Pace for 2015 | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="126" id="postImage_4047368743" src="http://img.scoop.it/3HcSJQfbi9oOrPIOCqdYNzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 126;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.cutimes.com/2015/07/05/data-breaches-on-record-pace-for-2015" onclick="trackPostClick(4047368743); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                   <wbr>

                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047368743/2015/07/09/data-breaches-on-record-pace-for-2015">

                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047368743">
                   <p>
                    <strong>
                     Data breaches in 2015 are on pace to break records both in the number of breaches and records exposed, the San Diego-based Identity Theft Resource Center said.In 2014
                    </strong>
                    , the number of U.S. data breaches tracked by ITRC hit a record high of 783, with 85,611,528 confirmed records exposed for 2014.
                   </p>

                   Kitchen printers or kitchen video display for your table service restaurant?
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.maitredpos.com/hospitality-epos-blog/roi-analysis-kitchen-printers-or-kitchen-video-display" onclick="trackPostClick(4047208114); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">

                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.maitredpos.com/hospitality-epos-blog/roi-analysis-kitchen-printers-or-kitchen-video-display" onclick="trackPostClick(4047208114); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">

                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047208114">
                   <blockquote>
                    Originally designed to handle fast food orders, kitchen video display systems have become increasingly common fixtures in fast food, casual and fine dining kitchens. Kitchen Display Systems eliminate steps, cut down on errors, improve productivity and speed of service, and drive increased guest satisfaction across all types and sizes of restaurants. Full color displays and multiple screen layouts make orders easy to read. The Bump Box is designed to make orders easy to control. And rich reporting keeps you on top of staff productivity at all times. With a Kitchen Display System, service is faster and more accurate, reports more detailed and complete, and end-of-day closings simplified: all at a significantly lower cost than printer, paper and ink.
                   </blockquote>

              <div class="ugc" data-lid="4047035225" data-tlid="2615592" data-viewmode="" id="post_4047035225">
               <div class="post-from postFrom">
                <table class="post-history posthistory">
                 <tr>
                  <td class="post-from-avatar">
                   <a class=" preview-profile" href="http://www.scoop.it/u/bob-frazier">

               <div class="post-view postView post-embed left medium ">
                <div class="rescoop-container">
                 <div class="rescoop">
                  <div class="button button-rescoop default " onclick="showSignupPopup(null, null, '?rescoop=4047035225');return false;" x-data-rescoop-onclick="showPostInScoopitWindow('/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047035225/2015/07/04/7-all-in-one-pos-must-haves/rescoop/2', null)">
                   <img src="/resources/img/post/icon_rescoop.png"/>
                   <span>
                    Scoop.it!
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4047035225">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/all-in-one-pos-must-haves-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4047035225 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   7 All-In-One POS Must-Haves
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/all-in-one-pos-must-haves-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4047035225); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="7 All-In-One POS Must-Haves | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="168" id="postImage_4047035225" src="http://img.scoop.it/qRe0UrajK-IN-h17bVCVOTl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 168;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/all-in-one-pos-must-haves-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4047035225); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .bsminfo
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4047035225/2015/07/04/7-all-in-one-pos-must-haves">
                    July 4, 5:22 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4047035225">
                   <blockquote>
                    Like their printer counterparts, an all-in-one POS (point of sale) system combines multiple technologies and integrates them into one housing to maximize value plus convenience to the end user. When talking about an all-in-one POS system, I am referring to a system that will conveniently deliver everything a business needs to begin processing customers. While many manufacturers herald some of their products as all-in-one, they often fall short and in fact do involve additional purchases and hassles. So what exactly should an all-in-one POS system have?
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046940973">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.restaurant.org/News-Research/News/To-EMV-or-not-to-EMV" onclick="trackPostClick(4046940973 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   To EMV or not to EMV?
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.restaurant.org/News-Research/News/To-EMV-or-not-to-EMV" onclick="trackPostClick(4046940973); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="To EMV or not to EMV? | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="112" id="postImage_4046940973" src="http://img.scoop.it/t5bCPvbvn_ZaiCZq9JYv3Tl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 112;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.restaurant.org/News-Research/News/To-EMV-or-not-to-EMV" onclick="trackPostClick(4046940973); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .restaurant
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .org
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046940973/2015/07/02/to-emv-or-not-to-emv">
                    July 2, 5:01 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046940973">
                   <p>
                    Deciding whether to invest in card-processing systems that accept credit and debit cards embedded with microchips  also known as EMV, or chip, cards -- is a hot topic in the restaurant world these days. Heres why: Starting Oct. 1, 2015, merchants who havent invested in EMV-enabled equipment will be liable for fraudulent purchases made with a counterfeit credit or debit card.If youre like many restaurateurs, you may be having a hard time building a business case to take action to meet the EMV liability shift. Often, the numbers just cant justify the time and cost it takes to implement the technology. As restaurants consider purchasing and installing EMV-enabled terminals, here are a few tips and pointers.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="post-curation-comment tCustomization tCustomization_post_comment_curation decorated ">
                 <div class="post-curation-comment-title">
                  Bob Frazier's insight:
                 </div>
                 <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description">
                  <p>
                   EMV for retail and QuickServ is ready, but there are still a lot of EMV issues with pre-authorizing Bar tabs and adding a tip for Table Service Restaurants! For
                   <a href="http://www.pos-advice.com/credit-card-fraud/" rel="nofollow" title="Link to EMV Blog Post ">
                    more EMV info
                   </a>
                   , read our blog post at
                   <a href="http://www.pos-advice.com/credit-card-fraud/" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.pos-advice.com/credit-card-fraud/
                   </a>
                   and watch the
                   <a href="http://www.pos-advice.com/video-library/" rel="nofollow" title="Link to What is EMV Video">
                    short video What is EMV?
                   </a>
                   at
                   <a href="http://www.pos-advice.com/video-library/" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.pos-advice.com/video-library/
                   </a>
                   .
                   <span>
                    For a weekly recap of restaurant management ideas, news, articles and info, subscribe to the free
                   </span>
                   <a href="http://pos-advicenewsletter.com/" rel="nofollow">
                    Restaurant Newsletter
                   </a>
                   <span>
                    at
                   </span>
                   <a href="http://pos-advicenewsletter.com/!" rel="nofollow">
                    http://pos-advicenewsletter.com/
                   </a>
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/ways-restaurant-owners-utilize-a-pos-to-enhance-their-customer-s-experience-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4046665740 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   6 Ways Restaurant Owners Utilize A POS To Enhance Their Customers Experience
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/ways-restaurant-owners-utilize-a-pos-to-enhance-their-customer-s-experience-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4046665740); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="6 Ways Restaurant Owners Utilize A POS To Enhance Their Customers Experience | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="149" id="postImage_4046665740" src="http://img.scoop.it/BmUkKg8Qu62mT-qN2SlTyzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 149;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://www.bsminfo.com/doc/ways-restaurant-owners-utilize-a-pos-to-enhance-their-customer-s-experience-0001" onclick="trackPostClick(4046665740); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   www
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .bsminfo
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046665740/2015/06/28/6-ways-restaurant-owners-utilize-a-pos-to-enhance-their-customer-s-experience">
                    June 28, 7:16 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046665740">
                   <blockquote>
                    Deploying a point of sale (POS) solution tailored to suit the restaurant business offers many benefits to owner/operators; from automating operations, streamlining communications, tracking inventory, and analyzing their business with a touch of a button. While the most commonly utilized features of a POS solution have helped restaurants increase revenue and boost profits, some owner/operators are looking beyond basic functionality and utilizing a combination of features to enhance the customer experience.
                   </blockquote>

                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046494524/2015/06/25/survey-results-chargers-are-the-new-wi-fi">
                    June 25, 7:28 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046494524">
                   <p>
                    We sent a survey to over 32,000 food and beverage industry professionalslast month, asking their thoughts on mobile charging solutions for customers. Since 2015 was deemed "the year of mobile," we knewwe would see an interest in in-venue smartphone charging in general. But we were really fired up by how many businesses stated that theyare likelyto implement charging services; the numbers are way beyond whatwe expected!Eighty-percent of U.S. adults now own smartphones and spend between 3.5 - 5.2 hours per day mobile multi-tasking.With customers spending over 50 percent of that time on their phones while in your place of business, it's inevitable that many of them will request a table near an outlet or ask the bartender or hostess to charge their phone. With so much online activity occurringin-venue,It's no wonder that dying or dead batteries have become a big problem for customers as well as business owners.Over fifty percent of managers we asked stated that their staff receive requests for smartphone charges over five times per day.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046441820">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/news/togo-s-eateries-improve-security-and-accountability-with-fingerprint-readers100799?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046441820 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Togo's Eateries Improve Security and Accountability with Fingerprint Readers
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/news/togo-s-eateries-improve-security-and-accountability-with-fingerprint-readers100799?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046441820); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="Togo's Eateries Improve Security and Accountability with Fingerprint Readers | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="165" id="postImage_4046441820" src="http://img.scoop.it/ksqDoxdDbtwJHvmnf1OaIDl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 165;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://hospitalitytechnology.edgl.com/news/togo-s-eateries-improve-security-and-accountability-with-fingerprint-readers100799?referaltype=newsletter" onclick="trackPostClick(4046441820); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   hospitalitytechno
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   logy
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .edgl
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046441820/2015/06/24/togo-s-eateries-improve-security-and-accountability-with-fingerprint-readers">
                    June 24, 3:36 PM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046441820">
                   <p>
                    Prior to biometrics, Togos POS system required employees to enter a password to sign in or authorize an override. However, management found it challenging to track access to the cash drawer because passwords can be shared. Today, more than 1,000 Togos employees use U.are.U 4500 USB fingerprint readers for simplified sign in. Fingerprint templates replace the need to enter a password, resulting in a unique and auditable identity for each transaction.The Crossmatch fingerprint readers are exceeding expectations at all levels for this restaurant chain. Franchisees like it because it enables auditable POS terminal access, transaction logs and time clock functions.
                   </p>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>

                    more Fingerprint ID info
                   </a>
                   visit
                   <a href="http://www.pos-advice.com/fingerprint-id-readers-a-valuable-pos-option/" rel="nofollow">
                    http://www.pos-advice.com/fingerprint-id-readers-a-valuable-pos-option/
                   </a>
                   .Where do bar owners, chefs and restaurateurs
                   <strong>
                    Find, Compare and Connect
                   </strong>
                   with the latest online and mobile technology? At
                   <a href="http://restaurantsoftwarelist.com/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    the Restaurant Software List website

                <div class="post-title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title editable-container tooltip-on-mouse" id="postTitle_4046416990">
                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://streetfightmag.com/2015/06/23/6-mobile-pre-ordering-tools-for-restaurants/?mc_cid=9d8e3cafaa&amp;mc_eid=1dd8be872d" onclick="trackPostClick(4046416990 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   6 Mobile Pre-Ordering Tools for Restaurants | Street Fight
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">
                  <a href="http://streetfightmag.com/2015/06/23/6-mobile-pre-ordering-tools-for-restaurants/?mc_cid=9d8e3cafaa&amp;mc_eid=1dd8be872d" onclick="trackPostClick(4046416990); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   <div class="thisistherealimage">
                    <img alt="6 Mobile Pre-Ordering Tools for Restaurants | Street Fight | Restaurant Technology | Scoop.it" class="postDisplayedImage" height="121" id="postImage_4046416990" src="http://img.scoop.it/fuSW66mOgkxOMlXYv-dHkzl72eJkfbmt4t8yenImKBVvK0kTmF0xjctABnaLJIm9" style="width:224; height: 121;" width="224"/>
                   </div>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-metas tCustomization_post_metas" style="margin-right: 25px; padding-bottom: 5px;">
                  From
                  <a href="http://streetfightmag.com/2015/06/23/6-mobile-pre-ordering-tools-for-restaurants/?mc_cid=9d8e3cafaa&amp;mc_eid=1dd8be872d" onclick="trackPostClick(4046416990); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   streetfightmag
                   <wbr>
                   </wbr>
                   .com
                  </a>
                  -
                  <span>
                   <a href="/t/restaurant-pos-by-bob-frazier-1/p/4046416990/2015/06/24/6-mobile-pre-ordering-tools-for-restaurants-street-fight">
                    June 24, 5:13 AM
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046416990">
                   <p>
                    Reservation apps have made it easier for customers to book tables at restaurants, and mobile ordering apps have shaved seconds off the time it takes to process transactions, but one of the biggest pain points in dining  the time customers spend waiting for food to be cooked and brought to their tables  hadnt been addressed until recently.Using mobile technology, vendors are now helping diners recapture the time they spend waiting for the food theyve paid for to be brought to their tables, while also improving operational efficiencies for partner restaurants. Here are six examples of apps that use mobile pre-ordering functionality to ensure piping hot dishes are ready-to-go immediately when customers arrive.
                   </p>
                  </div>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">
                  <a class=" title tCustomization tCustomization_post_title" href="http://www.atlantamagazine.com/dining-news/tired-of-waiting-for-the-check-new-app-dash-lets-diners-pay-or-split-the-tab/" onclick="trackPostClick(4046052384 ); return true;" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Tired of waiting for the check? New app, Dash, lets diners pay or split the tab
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                </div>
                <div class="post-content clearfix ">
                 <div class="post-image">

                 <div class="post-description editable-container tooltip-on-mouse">
                  <div class="tCustomization tCustomization_post_description" id="postDescription_4046052384">
                   <blockquote>
                    Flagging down an overwhelmed server or splitting the check among, say, sevenpeople is never a pleasantexperience. Thats why in November 2013, Jeff McGregor launched Dash, a free app that integrates with restaurant payment systems to allow diners to split and pay the bill. Already in New York, Chicago, and Washington, D.C., Dash launched in Atlanta yesterday, partneringwith more than 30 local restaurants.
                   </blockquote>
                  </div>

function linkedinShareSuccess(e) {

(function() {
    var po = document.createElement('script'); po.type = 'text/javascript'; po.async = true;
    po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';

function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}
}


function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);
